Last-Chance GPT Winners at Grand Prix London 2015
=================================================



 Posted in [GRAND PRIX LONDON 2015](/en/events/coverage/gplon15)
 on August 15, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/henke_author.jpg)
By Tobi Henke










While the main action may only start on Saturday, there definitely is quite a bit of action before then. For example, the Friday before a Grand Prix has hundreds of players competing in the last-chance Grand Prix Trials. This is the final opportunity for people to earn two byes for the main event and it's the first opportunity for us to get an early impression of what decks to expect this weekend. So let's take a look!







#### Ross Dibben, Grand Prix Trial Winner â€“ Grand Prix London 2015
